          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Prysmian is a global cabling solutions provider leading the energy transition and digital transformation. By leveraging its wide geographical footprint and extensive product range, its track record of technological leadership and innovation, and a strong customer base, the company is well-placed to capitalise on its leading positions and win in new, growing markets. Prysmian’s business strategy perfectly matches key market drivers by developing resilient, high-performing, sustainable and innovative cable solutions in the segments of Transmission, Power Grid, Electrification and Digital Solutions. Prysmian is a public company listed on the Italian Stock Exchange, with almost 150 years of experience, over 33,000 employees, 109 plants and 27 R&amp;D centres in over 50 countries, and sales of over €15 billion in 2023.

                      <icon class="ellipsis-menu__item-icon text-color-text h-[24px] w-[24px] mr-1" data-delayed-url="https://static.licdn.com/aero-v1/sc/h/iq0x9q37wj214o129ai1yjut">

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The CIGRE 2025 International Symposium in Montréal, Canada has come to an end.

<a class="link" href="https://it.linkedin.com/in/cinzia-faris%C3%A8-a2000751?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cinzia Farisè</a>, Executive Vice President Power Grid and Electrification at Prysmian joined the business panel “Navigating Business and Supply Chain Challenges in the Energy Transition” to provide - together with global industry leaders - a perspective of the energy transition impacts on global supply chains.

 A few highlights from her contribution to the discussion:

 ⚡️“Partnership and innovation are not just a fundamental part of who we are. We firmly believe that they are key factors to ensure continuity and optimisation of the entire supply chain, which is one of our strategic priorities."

 💡 "Grids are evolving at a very fast pace and are expressing new needs and new challenges. To provide answers to such new needs and accelerate the energy transition, the grid should become an inclusive platform where all the stakeholders reinforce the commitment of working together in boosting the power grid ecosystem."

 👥 ”Empowerment and engagement are key to make the difference. We are investing selectively in new lines, to increase our capacity, but not only. We invest in People to build and develop the right skills in the direct and indirect grid value chain. We have just inaugurated the Prysmian Power Grid Academy, to build our sustainable leaders of the energy transition."

We thank HydroQuebec for hosting the Symposium. Prysmian has been a very proud partner to HydroQuebec for many years. We have a shared spirit of innovation, and we feel proud to have been at their side for their challenges over the years.</p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We’re excited to announce that we have been selected as the preferred bidder for the high voltage (HVDC) cable interconnector project ‘Eastern Green Link 4’ by the GB transmission owners, SP Transmission plc and National Grid Electricity Transmission plc.

The project, which will run between Scotland and England, via a route in the North Sea, will play a central role in further enhancing the energy security of the United Kingdom. Eastern Green Link 4 will be part of future proofing the British energy grid while facilitating the transition to clean and more affordable energy.

Prysmian has a long history of delivering major interconnectors in the UK, including the Eastern Green Link 1 &amp; 2 projects and the Viking Link interconnector, which is the longest land and subsea high voltage cable interconnector in the world. 

Read more at: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dPpRfGWA?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dPpRfGWA</a> </p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We are delighted to announce that <a class="link" href="https://it.linkedin.com/in/cinzia-faris%C3%A8-a2000751?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cinzia Farisè</a>, Executive Vice President Power Grid and Electrification for Prysmian, will join the business panel “Navigating Business and Supply Chain Challenges in the Energy Transition”  at the CIGRE 2025 International Symposium hosted by HydroQuebec on September 30 in Montréal, Canada.

The panel brings together global thought leaders and industry pioneers for a high-impact discussion on the complexities and opportunities presented by the global shift toward sustainable energy. The session will explore strategic approaches to overcoming supply chain disruptions and leveraging innovation to drive business growth in the evolving energy landscape.

“I look forward to this year’s CIGRE Symposium and the opportunity to share the stage alongside my colleagues in this space,” said Farisè. “It will be a worthwhile discussion about the unique ways we are tackling supply chain challenges while the grid has to become an inclusive platform where we reinforce the commitment of innovating together, as we continue to lead the energy transition in our industry.”

Discover more: <a class="link" href="https://cigre.ca/2025/en/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://cigre.ca/2025/en/</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">On September 25th, representatives from the HR team and the Installation Marine Department of Prysmian Powerlink visited the Genoa Shipping Academy, an institution with which we have a partnership for the recruitment of specific maritime roles.

The meeting was a valuable opportunity to gain deeper insight into the dynamics of the Academy, discover its new facilities, and explore the academic and professional developments it is leading. It also allowed us to evaluate potential future collaborations aimed at strengthening Prysmian’s visibility and attracting new talent.
</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Een grote handtekening voor een groot project: Zuid-West 380kV Oost
 
Prysmian Nederland levert de kabels voor het project Zuid-West 380kV Oost, de nieuwe 380kV-verbinding tussen Rilland en Tilburg. Dit grootschalige infrastructuurproject van <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/tennettso?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>TenneT</a> wordt gerealiseerd in samenwerking met een indrukwekkende groep partners.
Samen met <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/baminfra?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>BAM Infra Nederland</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/strukton-wegen-beton?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Strukton Wegen &amp; Beton</a>, <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/hanab-energy-solutions?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hanab Energy Solutions</a>, <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/hanab?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hanab</a>, <a class="link" href="https://fr.linkedin.com/company/spie_2?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SPIE</a>, <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/qirion?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Qirion</a> en vele andere betrokken partijen zetten we ons in voor een veilige, efficiënte en goed afgestemde uitvoering van dit project.
 
Namens <a class="link" href="https://it.linkedin.com/company/prysmian?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Prysmian</a> was <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/in/martijn-sterk-0a131b52?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Martijn Sterk</a>, Project Manager, aanwezig bij het officiële ondertekenmoment van de coördinatieovereenkomsten — een belangrijke stap richting de realisatie.
 
Met deze samenwerking zorgen we ervoor dat de werkzaamheden goed op elkaar zijn afgestemd en dat de impact op de omgeving tot een minimum wordt beperkt. We kijken uit naar een succesvolle uitvoering van dit project, dat bijdraagt aan een toekomstbestendig energienet.
 
<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fprysmian&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Prysmian</a> <a class="link" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#TenneT</a> <a class="link"
